      data node2 {
      

      6
      	int val;
      

      7

      10
      /*
      

      11
      	- complete binary tree: 
      

      12
      		- a binary tree in which every level, except possibly the deepest is completely filled;
      

      13
      		- at depth n, the height of the tree, all nodes are as far left as possible.
      

      14
      */
      

      15
      

      16
      /* the view that we used:
      

      17
       	- n is the height
      

      18
      	- nmin is the "minim height" 
      

      19
      		- is the length of the shortest path to a leaf (the minimum between the heights for the two children) 
      

      20
      		- we used it to make the insertion easier (because in the insertion there are points where we need to
      

      21
      		know if a subtree is perfect or not)
      

      22
      */
      

      23
      

      24
      complete == self = null & n = 0 & nmin = 0
      

      25
      	or self::node2<_, l, r> * l::complete * r::complete & nmin = min(nmin1, nmin2) + 1
      

      26
      	or self::node2<_, l, r> * l::complete * r::complete & nmin = min(nmin1, nmin2) + 1
      

      27
      	inv nmin >= 0 & n >= nmin;
      

      28
      

      29
      /*complete == 
      

      30
        self = null & n = 0 & nmin = 0
      

      31
      	or self::node2<_, l, r> * l::complete * r::complete & nmin = n
      

      32
      	or self::node2<_, l, r> * l::complete * r::complete & nmin = n-1
      

      33
        or self::node2<_, l, r> * l::complete * r::complete & nmin = n-1
      

      34
        or self::node2<_, l, r> * l::complete * r::complete & nmin = n-1
      

      35
      	inv nmin >= 0 & n >= nmin;*/
      

      36
      

      37
      int maxim(int a, int b) 
      

      38
      	requires true
      

      39
      	ensures (a < b | res = a) & (a >= b | res = b);
      

      40
      {
      

      41
      	if(a >= b)
      

      42
      		return a;
      

      43
      	else
      

      44
      		return b;
      

      45
      }
      

      46
      

      47
      int minim(int a, int b) 
      

      48
      	requires true
      

      49
      	ensures (a < b | res = b) & (a >= b | res = a);
      

      50
      {
      

      51
      	if(a >= b)
      

      52
      		return b;
      

      53
      	else
      

      54
      		return a;
      

      55
      }
      

      56
      

      57
      int height(node2 t) 
      

      58
      	requires t::complete
      

      59
      	ensures t::complete & res = n;
      

      60
      {
      

      61
      	if (t != null)
      

      62
      		return maxim(height(t.left), height(t.right)) + 1;
      

      63
      	else return 0;
      

      64
      }
      

      65
      

      66
      int min_height(node2 t) 
      

      67
      	requires t::complete
      

      68
      	ensures t::complete & res = nmin;
      

      69
      {
      

      70
      	if (t != null)
      

      71
      		return minim(min_height(t.left), min_height(t.right)) + 1;
      

      72
      	else return 0;
      

      73
      }
      

      74
      

      75
      void insert(ref node2 t, int v)
      

      76
      	requires t::complete & nmin < n // there is still place to insert
      

      77
      	ensures t'::complete & (nmin1 = nmin | nmin1 = nmin + 1);  
      

      78
      	requires t::complete & nmin = n // there is no empty place -> we need to increase the height
      

      79
      	ensures t'::complete & (nmin1 = nmin | nmin1 = nmin + 1);  
      

      80
      {
      

      81
      	node2 aux;
      

      82
      	
      

      83
      	if(t == null) {
      

      84
      		t = new node2(v, null, null);	
      

      85
      		return;	
      

      86
      	}
      

      87
      	else {
      

      88
      		if(min_height(t.left) < height(t.left)) {		// there is still space in the left subtree
      

      89
            aux = t.left;
      

      90
      			insert(aux, v);
      

      91
      			t.left = aux;
      

      92
      			return;	
      

      93
      		}
      

      94
      		else {
      

      95
            if(min_height(t.right) < height(t.right)) {	// there is still space in the right subtree
      

      96
              aux = t.right;
      

      97
      				insert(aux, v);
      

      98
      				t.right = aux;
      

      99
      				return;	
      

      100
      			}
      

      101
      			else {
      

      102
      				node2 tmp = t.right;
      

      103
            	if(height(t.left) == height(t.right)) { // tree is full - we must start another level 
      

      104
      					aux = t.left;
      

      105
      					insert(aux, v);
      

      106
      					t.left = aux;
      

      107
      					return;	
      

      108
      				}
      

      109
      				else {
      

      110
                aux = t.right;    
      

      111
      					insert(aux, v);
      

      112
                t.right = aux;
      

      113
      					return;	
      

      114
      				}
      

      115
      			}
      

      116
      		}
      

      117
      	}
      

      118
      }
